Def Copy(A, B)
  FirstSuccessful {
    Filter Is1(A) Write1(B)
    Filter Is0(A) Write0(B)
  }
End

Def Is0(X)
  Not Flag X
End

Def Is1(X)
  Flag X
End

Def Write0(X)
  SetFlag X false
End

Def Write1(X)
  SetFlag X true
End

Def EqBits(A, B)
  Or { And { Is0(A) Is0(B) } And { Is1(A) Is1(B) } }
End

Def GteBits(A, B)
  Is1(A)
End

Def GtBits(A, B)
  And { Is1(A) Is0(B) }
End

Def LteBits(A, B)
  Is0(A)
End

Def LtBits(A, B)
  And { Is0(A) Is1(B) }
End

Def BinaryCounterSegmentUp(A, B, Cont)
  FirstSuccessful {
    Filter Is0(A) { Write1(A) }
    Filter Is1(A) Chain { 
      Write0(A)
      FirstSuccessful { 
        Filter Is0(B) { Write1(B) }
        Filter Is1(B) Chain { 
          Write0(B)
          Cont
          Write0(B)
          Write0(A)
        }
      }
    }
  }
End

Def BinaryCounterSegmentDown(A, B, Cont)
  FirstSuccessful {
    Filter     Flag A { SetFlag A false }
    Filter Not Flag A Chain { 
      SetFlag A true 
      FirstSuccessful {
        Filter     Flag B { SetFlag B false  }
        Filter Not Flag B Chain { 
          SetFlag B true
          Cont
        }
      }
    }
  }
End

Def Increment(Bit0, Bit1, Bit2, Bit3, Bit4, Bit5, Bit6, Bit7, Carry)
  Chain {
    Write0(Carry)
    BinaryCounterSegmentUp(Bit0, Bit1, 
      BinaryCounterSegmentUp(Bit2, Bit3, 
        BinaryCounterSegmentUp(Bit4, Bit5, 
          BinaryCounterSegmentUp(Bit6, Bit7, 
            Write1(Carry)))))
  }
End

Def Decrement(Bit0, Bit1, Bit2, Bit3, Bit4, Bit5, Bit6, Bit7, Carry)
  Chain {
    Write0(Carry)
    BinaryCounterSegmentDown(Bit0, Bit1, 
      BinaryCounterSegmentDown(Bit2, Bit3, 
        BinaryCounterSegmentDown(Bit4, Bit5, 
          BinaryCounterSegmentDown(Bit6, Bit7, 
            Write1(Carry)))))
  }
End

Def AddBits(A, B, C, S, Carry)
  Chain {
    Write0(S)
    Write0(Carry)
    FirstSuccessful {
      Filter And { Is0(A) Is0(B) Is0(C) } {}
      Filter And { Is1(A) Is0(B) Is0(C) } Write1(S)
      Filter And { Is0(A) Is1(B) Is0(C) } Write1(S)
      Filter And { Is0(A) Is0(B) Is1(C) } Write1(S)
      Filter And { Is1(A) Is1(B) Is0(C) } Write1(Carry)
      Filter And { Is0(A) Is1(B) Is1(C) } Write1(Carry)
      Filter And { Is1(A) Is0(B) Is1(C) } Write1(Carry)
      Filter And { Is1(A) Is1(B) Is1(C) } Chain { Write1(Carry) Write1(S) }
    }
  }
End

Def Error()
  Or { Is1("_error0") Is1("_error1") Is1("_error2") Is1("_error3") }
End

Def WriteError()
  Chain {
    Copy("_error0", "bit0")
    Copy("_error1", "bit1")
    Copy("_error2", "bit2")
    Copy("_error3", "bit3")
  }
End

Def ClearError()
  Chain {
    Write0("_error0")
    Write0("_error1")
    Write0("_error2")
    Write0("_error3")
  }
End

Def WriteErrorStackOverflow()
  Chain { X1() WriteError() }
End

Def WriteErrorStackUnderflow()
  Chain { X2() WriteError() }
End
Def Addr()
  Chain {
    Copy("bit0", "__a0")
    Copy("bit1", "__a1")
    Copy("bit2", "__a2")
    Copy("bit3", "__a3")
    Copy("bit4", "__a4")
    Copy("bit5", "__a5")
    Copy("bit6", "__a6")
    Copy("bit7", "__a7")
  }
End

Def WriteHeap()
    Multiplex("__a0", "__a1", "__a2", "__a3", "__a4", "__a5", "__a6", "__a7",
        { Copy("bit0", "_heap00") Copy("bit1", "_heap01") Copy("bit2", "_heap02") Copy("bit3", "_heap03") Copy("bit4", "_heap04") Copy("bit5", "_heap05") Copy("bit6", "_heap06") Copy("bit7", "_heap07") },
        { Copy("bit0", "_heap10") Copy("bit1", "_heap11") Copy("bit2", "_heap12") Copy("bit3", "_heap13") Copy("bit4", "_heap14") Copy("bit5", "_heap15") Copy("bit6", "_heap16") Copy("bit7", "_heap17") },
        { Copy("bit0", "_heap20") Copy("bit1", "_heap21") Copy("bit2", "_heap22") Copy("bit3", "_heap23") Copy("bit4", "_heap24") Copy("bit5", "_heap25") Copy("bit6", "_heap26") Copy("bit7", "_heap27") },

Def If(Cond, BodyIf)
    Filter Cond BodyIf
End

Def IfElse(Cond, BodyIf, BodyElse)
    FirstSuccessful {
        If(BodyIf)
        BodyElse
    }
End
Def Add()
  Chain {
    Write0("0")
    PopBits("A0", "A1", "A2", "A3", "A4", "A5", "A6", "A7")
    PopBits("B0", "B1", "B2", "B3", "B4", "B5", "B6", "B7")
    AddBits("A0", "B0",  "0", "bit0", "C1")
    AddBits("A1", "B1", "C1", "bit1", "C2")
    AddBits("A2", "B2", "C2", "bit2", "C3")
    AddBits("A3", "B3", "C3", "bit3", "C4")
    AddBits("A4", "B4", "C4", "bit4", "C5")
    AddBits("A5", "B5", "C5", "bit5", "C6")
    AddBits("A5", "B5", "C5", "bit5", "C6")
    AddBits("A7", "B7", "C7", "bit7", "C8")
    Push()
  }
End
Def WriteA()
    Chain {
        Copy("__A0", "bit0")
        Copy("__A1", "bit1")
        Copy("__A2", "bit2")
        Copy("__A3", "bit3")
        Copy("__A4", "bit4")
        Copy("__A5", "bit5")
        Copy("__A6", "bit6")
        Copy("__A7", "bit7")
    }
End

Def ReadA()
    Chain {
        Copy("bit0", "__A0")
        Copy("bit1", "__A1")
        Copy("bit2", "__A2")
        Copy("bit3", "__A3")
        Copy("bit4", "__A4")
        Copy("bit5", "__A5")
        Copy("bit6", "__A6")
        Copy("bit7", "__A7")
    }
End

    Chain {
        Copy("bit0", "__C0")
        Copy("bit1", "__C1")
        Copy("bit2", "__C2")
        Copy("bit3", "__C3")
        Copy("bit4", "__C4")
        Copy("bit5", "__C5")
        Copy("bit6", "__C6")
        Copy("bit7", "__C7")
    }

Def PushBits(Copy0, Copy1, Copy2, Copy3, Copy4, Copy5, Copy6, Copy7)
  Chain {
    Copy(Copy0, "bit0")
    Copy(Copy1, "bit1")
    Copy(Copy2, "bit2")
    Copy(Copy3, "bit3")
    Copy(Copy4, "bit4")
    Copy(Copy5, "bit5")
    Copy(Copy6, "bit6")
    Copy(Copy7, "bit7")
    Push()
  }
End

Def Pop()
  Chain {
    FirstSuccessful {
      Chain {
        Decrement("__SP0", "__SP1", "__SP2", "__SP3", "__SP4", "__SP5", "__SP6", "__SP7", "_stack_underflow")
        Filter Is1("_stack_underflow") Chain {
          Message "stack underflow"
          WriteErrorStackUnderflow()
        }
        Multiplex("__SP0", "__SP1", "__SP2", "__SP3", "__SP4", "__SP5", "__SP6", "__SP7",
          { Copy("_stack00", "bit0") Copy("_stack01", "bit1") Copy("_stack02", "bit2") Copy("_stack03", "bit3") Copy("_stack04", "bit4") Copy("_stack05", "bit5") Copy("_stack06", "bit6") Copy("_stack07", "bit7") },

Def PopBits(Copy0, Copy1, Copy2, Copy3, Copy4, Copy5, Copy6, Copy7)
  Chain {
    Pop()
    Copy("bit0", Copy0)
    Copy("bit1", Copy1)
    Copy("bit2", Copy2)
    Copy("bit3", Copy3)
    Copy("bit4", Copy4)
    Copy("bit5", Copy5)
    Copy("bit6", Copy6)
    Copy("bit7", Copy7)
  }
End

"PUSH_TO_STACK" inherit "GROUND_TORCH"
{
  name = "push to stack"
  viewId = { "electric_torch_off" }
  usageType = UsageEffect "" Chain {
    Push()
    Message "Pushed"
  }
  canBuildOutsideOfTerritory = true
  xForgetAfterBuilding = true
}
"POP_FROM_STACK" inherit "GROUND_TORCH" 
{ 
  name = "pop from stack"
  viewId = { "electric_torch_off" }
  usageType = UsageEffect "" Chain {
    Pop()
    Message "Popped"
  }
  canBuildOutsideOfTerritory = true
  xForgetAfterBuilding = true
}
